[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika M3U8Parser component. The parser attempts to establish an outbound network [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m` when processing M3U8 playlist content, which is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered by untrusted input data. This vulnerability is classified as a medium [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseverity security issue that could potentially lead to exfiltration of sensitive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata or exposure of internal services.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability detected [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the Jazzer fuzzing framework's security sanitizers. The vulnerability occurs [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring the parsing of M3U8 playlist files by Apache Tika's M3U8Parser.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `[0m[1;35mM3U8ParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which calls [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mM3U8Parser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is invoked, which internally calls `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. During parsing, the `[0m[1;35mM3U8Parser.handleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is executed at line [0m[1;36m170[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This triggers `[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operations at lines [0m[1;36m570[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m606[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mURLConnection.getContentType[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method attempts to retrieve content type [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minformation[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. This initiates an HTTP connection through `HttpURLConnection` which ultimately [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to establish a socket connection[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. The Jazzer SSRF sanitizer detects and blocks the connection attempt to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability type is Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which occurs when an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication can be manipulated to make requests to destinations based on untrusted [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput data. In this case, the M3U8 parser appears to be processing URLs embedded [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin M3U8 playlist content and attempting to fetch resources from those URLs [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout proper validation or restrictions.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The connection attempt is made to an external domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that the parser is processing URLs from the input content[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability is triggered through the `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mM3U8Parser, suggesting that the parser follows references in playlist files[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The use of `[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with `[0m[1;35mURLConnection.getContentType[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates that Tika is attempting to automatically detect content types by fetching[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote resources[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability allows untrusted input to control network destinations, which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis the core characteristic of SSRF vulnerabilities[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a holistic view of this issue, the following parts of the codebase should[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe investigated:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8Parser` - specifically the `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m170[0m[39m, `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m92[0m[39m, and `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m77[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.io.TikaInputStream` - the `[0m[1;35mget[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods at lines [0m[1;36m570[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m606[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto understand how URLs are processed and fetched[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The M3U8 file format handling logic to understand what types of URLs or links [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare extracted from playlist files[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Input validation and sanitization mechanisms [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor lack thereof[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for URLs [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted from M3U8 content[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Configuration options or settings that might control whether the parser should [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollow external references[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Other parser implementations in Apache Tika that might exhibit similar behavior [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen handling external references[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"RSS parse error"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for M3U8Parser SSRF Vulnerability[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Issue Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability in M3U8Parser stems from the automatic fetching of HTTP URLs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted from untrusted M3U8 playlist content. The vulnerability occurs in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at lines [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m174[0m[39m, where:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. URLs are extracted from M3U8 playlist files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m156[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. URLs starting with [0m[32m"http"[0m[39m trigger automatic resource fetching [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m164[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` establishes a network connection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The connection happens BEFORE any security validation can prevent it[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Even the `[0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check at line [0m[1;36m169[0m[39m is ineffective because the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection is established during try-with-resources initialization[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Root Cause[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fundamental problem is that the parser treats URLs from untrusted input as safe[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresources to fetch automatically. The `[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m598[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls `[0m[1;35murl.openConnection[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unconditionally, and line [0m[1;36m606[0m[39m calls [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mconnection.getContentType[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which triggers the actual network request. This [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhappens before any application-level security checks can intervene.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Evidence from Codebase Analysis[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSeveral key findings support the fix strategy:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**From Test Analysis:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The M3U8ParserTest only validates metadata extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mduration, playlist links, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion, playlist type[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The test file uses relative URLs [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"entire1.ts"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not HTTP URLs[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- There are NO tests that verify or require HTTP URL fetching functionality[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This proves that automatic HTTP fetching is NOT a core requirement[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**From Similar Parsers:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **FeedParser** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m109[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m112[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Extracts URLs from RSS/Atom feeds but does NOT [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetch them - treats URLs as textual content only[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **OfflineContentHandler**: Demonstrates Tika's established pattern for preventing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal resource access in XML parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTIKA-[0m[1;36m185[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both parsers show that Tika can safely handle URLs without automatically fetching[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**From Configuration Patterns:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- DocumentSelector pattern exists but is ineffective here because it's checked [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAFTER connection establishment[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The check should occur BEFORE creating TikaInputStream, not during resource usage[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Recommended Fix Strategy[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSafest and Simplest[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the automatic HTTP URL fetching behavior from the `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserve lines [0m[1;36m153[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m163[0m[39m**: Keep the URL extraction and metadata storage logic[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This maintains core functionality: extracting playlist information[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The URL is still recorded in metadata via `[0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Remove lines [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m174[0m[39m**: Delete the entire HTTP fetching block[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the EmbeddedDocumentExtractor logic[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Optional Enhancement**: Add the URL as a link in XHTML output [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfollowing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFeedParser pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After line [0m[1;36m163[0m[39m, add XHTML output similar to FeedParser lines [0m[1;36m111[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m114[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create an anchor element with the URL as href attribute[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves the URL information in the parsed output without fetching it[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Modified [0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method structure:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLines [0m[1;36m153[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m163[0m[39m: Keep unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL extraction and metadata storage[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLine [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m174[0m[39m: REMOVE entirely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP fetching block[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOptional: Add XHTML link output after line [0m[1;36m163[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLine [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m: Keep [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclosing brace[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the vulnerability completely**: No network connections are made to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted URLs[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Maintains core functionality**: Metadata extraction still works [0m[1;39m([0m[39mproven by [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting test[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Tika patterns**: Aligns with FeedParser and OfflineContentHandler [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproaches[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward compatible**: Existing tests pass; only removes untested behavior[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Defense in depth**: Removes the attack surface entirely rather than adding [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation layers[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Minimal code changes**: Simple deletion reduces risk of introducing new bugs[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why more complex solutions are NOT needed:**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **URL validation approach**: Would be complex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchecking for private IPs, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal domains, scheme restrictions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and could be bypassed[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Configuration flag approach**: Adds complexity and still requires URL [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation; default-off breaks potential [0m[1;39m([0m[39muntested[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use cases[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Moving [0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m check**: Still requires URL validation to prevent[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF to internal resources[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. URL extraction continues to work [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m156[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Metadata storage continues to work [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The [0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method's line-by-line processing continues unchanged[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Duration, version, and playlist type extraction remain intact[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. All existing tests continue to pass[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Impact:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who rely on automatic HTTP URL fetching from M3U8 playlists will lose this [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- However, this behavior is:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Not covered by tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39msuggesting it's not widely used[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A security vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaking it harmful to retain[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Not part of the documented core functionality[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The URLs are still extracted and stored in metadata[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who need the embedded content can:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Extract URLs from metadata[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Fetch them separately with proper security controls[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Use their own validation and allowlist mechanisms[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No breaking changes to:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Core parsing functionality[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Metadata extraction[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test suite[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other parser behaviors[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFrom the initial codebase:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Open file: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-audio[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvideo-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/m3/M3U8Parser.java`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m153[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Delete lines [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m174[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe entire HTTP fetching block[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the early return[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the EmbeddedDocumentExtractor retrieval[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the Metadata creation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the shouldParseEmbedded check[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the try-with-resources block with [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The method should end immediately after line [0m[1;36m163[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Optional: Add XHTML link output after line [0m[1;36m163[0m[39m to preserve URL information in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed output [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimilar to FeedParser[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verify the method structure matches the safe pattern used by FeedParser[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Code Context Preservation[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix maintains all critical logic:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- M3U8 format parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m[39m in _parse method[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- EXTINF directive handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m92[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Duration extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Version extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m96[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m99[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Encryption detection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m101[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Playlist type extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m106[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- URL extraction and metadata storage [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m156[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe only removed functionality is the automatic fetching of HTTP URLs, which is the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF vulnerability itself.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
